(********************************************************************

 Construction of cartesian monoidal categories

 Every category with binary products and a terminal object gives rise
 to a monoidal category.

 Contents
 1. Construction of cartesian monoidal categories
 2. Properties of cartesian monoidal categories
 3. Cartesian closed categories
 4. Set as cartesian monoidal category
 5. Useful lemmas

Note: after refactoring on March 10, 2023, the prior Git history of this development is found via
git log -- UniMath/CategoryTheory/Monoidal/CartesianMonoidalCategoriesWhiskered.v

 ********************************************************************)

(**
 1. Construction of cartesian monoidal categories
 *)
Section GeneralConstruction.
  Context (C : category)
          (CP : BinProducts C)
          (terminal : Terminal C).

  
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
bifunctor_data C C C

C → C → C

CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
∏ b a1 a2 : C, C ⟦ a1, a2 ⟧ → C ⟦ ?F a1 b, ?F a2 b ⟧

∏ a b : C,
BinProductOfArrows C (CP a b) (CP a b) (identity a)
  (identity b) = identity (CP a b)
C: category

  (CP a b) (identity a) 
  (identity b) = identity (CP a b)
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
∏ (a b1 b2 b3 : C) (g1 : C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧)
(g2 : C ⟦ b2, b3 ⟧),
BinProductOfArrows C (CP a b3) 
  (CP a b1) (identity a) 
  (g1 · g2) =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP a b2) 
  (CP a b1) (identity a) g1
· BinProductOfArrows C 
    (CP a b3) (CP a b2) 
    (identity a) g2
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
∏ (b a1 a2 a3 : C) (f1 : C ⟦ a1, a2 ⟧)
(f2 : C ⟦ a2, a3 ⟧),
BinProductOfArrows C (CP a3 b) 
  (CP a1 b) (f1 · f2) (identity b) =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP a2 b) 
  (CP a1 b) f1 (identity b)
· BinProductOfArrows C 
    (CP a3 b) (CP a2 b) f2 
    (identity b)
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
∏ (a1 a2 b1 b2 : C) (f : C ⟦ a1, a2 ⟧)
(g : C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧),
f ⊗^{ tensorfrombinprod_data} g =
functoronmorphisms2 tensorfrombinprod_data f g

BinProductPr1 C (CP b c)
C: category

  (identity c) · BinProductPr2 C (CP b c) =
BinProductPr2 C (CP b c)

      
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C

BinProductOfArrows C (CP b c) (CP b c) (identity b)
  (identity c) · BinProductPr1 C (CP b c) =
BinProductPr1 C (CP b c)
 now rewrite BinProductOfArrowsPr1, id_right.

C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
∏ (a b1 b2 b3 : C) (g1 : C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧)
(g2 : C ⟦ b2, b3 ⟧),
BinProductOfArrows C (CP a b3) (CP a b1) (identity a)
  (g1 · g2) =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP a b2) (CP a b1) (identity a)
  g1
· BinProductOfArrows C (CP a b3) (CP a b2)
    (identity a) g2
 
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
b, c1, c2, c3: C
g1: C ⟦ c1, c2 ⟧
g2: C ⟦ c2, c3 ⟧
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b c3) (CP b c1) (identity b)
  (g1 · g2) =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b c2) (CP b c1) (identity b)
  g1
· BinProductOfArrows C (CP b c3) (CP b c2)
    (identity b) g2

      now rewrite BinProductOfArrows_comp, id_right.
    
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
∏ (b a1 a2 a3 : C) (f1 : C ⟦ a1, a2 ⟧)
(f2 : C ⟦ a2, a3 ⟧),
BinProductOfArrows C (CP a3 b) (CP a1 b) (f1 · f2)
  (identity b) =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP a2 b) (CP a1 b) f1
  (identity b)
· BinProductOfArrows C (CP a3 b) (CP a2 b) f2
    (identity b)
 
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
b1, b2, b3, c: C
f1: C ⟦ b2, b3 ⟧
f2: C ⟦ b3, c ⟧
BinProductOfArrows C (CP c b1) (CP b2 b1) (f1 · f2)
  (identity b1) =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b3 b1) (CP b2 b1) f1
  (identity b1)
· BinProductOfArrows C (CP c b1) (CP b3 b1) f2
    (identity b1)

      now rewrite BinProductOfArrows_comp, id_right.
    
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
∏ (a1 a2 b1 b2 : C) (f : C ⟦ a1, a2 ⟧)
(g : C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧),
f ⊗^{ tensorfrombinprod_data} g =
functoronmorphisms2 tensorfrombinprod_data f g
 
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
b1, b2, c1, c2: C
f: C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ c1, c2 ⟧
f ⊗^{ tensorfrombinprod_data} g =
functoronmorphisms2 tensorfrombinprod_data f g

      
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
b1, b2, c1, c2: C
f: C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ c1, c2 ⟧
f ⊗^{ tensorfrombinprod_data}_{r} c1
· b2 ⊗^{ tensorfrombinprod_data}_{l} g =
b1 ⊗^{ tensorfrombinprod_data}_{l} g
· f ⊗^{ tensorfrombinprod_data}_{r} c2

      
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
b1, b2, c1, c2: C
f: C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ c1, c2 ⟧
(pr22 tensorfrombinprod_data) c1 b1 b2 f
· (pr12 tensorfrombinprod_data) b2 c1 c2 g =
(pr12 tensorfrombinprod_data) b1 c1 c2 g
· (pr22 tensorfrombinprod_data) c2 b1 b2 f

      
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
b1, b2, c1, c2: C
f: C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ c1, c2 ⟧
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b2 c1) (CP b1 c1) f
  (identity c1)
· BinProductOfArrows C (CP b2 c2) (CP b2 c1)
    (identity b2) g =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b1 c2) (CP b1 c1)
  (identity b1) g
· BinProductOfArrows C (CP b2 c2) (CP b1 c2) f
    (identity c2)

      
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
b1, b2, c1, c2: C
f: C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ c1, c2 ⟧
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b2 c2) (CP b1 c1)
  (f · identity b2) (identity c1 · g) =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b2 c2) (CP b1 c1)
  (identity b1 · f) (g · identity c2)

      
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
b1, b2, c1, c2: C
f: C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ c1, c2 ⟧
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b2 c2) (CP b1 c1) f
  (identity c1 · g) =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b2 c2) (CP b1 c1)
  (identity b1 · f) g

      
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
b1, b2, c1, c2: C
f: C ⟦ b1, b2 ⟧
g: C ⟦ c1, c2 ⟧
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b2 c2) (CP b1 c1) f g =
BinProductOfArrows C (CP b2 c2) (CP b1 c1) f g

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

      · BinProductArrow C (CP b (CP c d))
          (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP b c) d)
           · BinProductPr1 C (CP b c))
          (BinProductArrow C (CP c d)
             (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP b c) d)
              · BinProductPr2 C (CP b c))
             (BinProductPr2 C (CP (CP b c) d)))))
· BinProductPr1 C (CP a (CP b (CP c d))) =

  (BinProductArrow C (CP (CP a b) (CP c d))
     (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP (CP a b) c) d)
      · BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP a b) c))
     (BinProductArrow C (CP c d)
        (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP (CP a b) c) d)
         · BinProductPr2 C (CP (CP a b) c))
        (BinProductPr2 C (CP (CP (CP a b) c) d)))
   · (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP a b) (CP c d))
      · BinProductPr1 C (CP a b)))

     (BinProductArrow C (CP c d)

        (BinProductPr2 C (CP (CP (CP a b) c) d)))

        · BinProductPr1 C (CP a b))
       (BinProductArrow C (CP b c)
          (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP a b) c)
           · BinProductPr2 C (CP a b))
          (BinProductPr2 C (CP (CP a b) c))))
  (BinProductPr2 C (CP (CP (CP a b) c) d) · identity d)
· (BinProductArrow C (CP (CP b c) d)
     (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP a (CP b c)) d)
      · BinProductPr2 C (CP a (CP b c)))
     (BinProductPr2 C (CP (CP a (CP b c)) d))
   · (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP b c) d)
      · BinProductPr1 C (CP b c))) = ?b

     (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP a (CP b c)) d)
      · BinProductPr2 C (CP a (CP b c)))
     (BinProductPr2 C (CP (CP a (CP b c)) d))
   · (BinProductPr1 C (CP (CP b c) d)
      · BinProductPr2 C (CP b c))) = ?b

        (unfold semi_cart_tensor_pr1 ; cbn ;
         unfold monoidal_cat_tensor_mor ;

         rewrite id_right ;

     symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat,

C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
expC: Exponentials CP
∏
x y
 z : cartesian_monoidalcat,,
     symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat,
(cartesian_monoidalcat,,
 symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat)
⟦ monoidal_cat_tensor_pt z x, y ⟧

  (λ x0 : cartesian_monoidalcat,,

   exp (expC x0)) x y ⟧

C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
expC: Exponentials CP
∏
(x y
 z : cartesian_monoidalcat,,
     symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat)
(f : (cartesian_monoidalcat,,
      symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat)
     ⟦ monoidal_cat_tensor_pt z x, y ⟧),
monoidal_cat_tensor_mor
  ((λ (x0 y0
       z0 : cartesian_monoidalcat,,
            symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat)
    (f0 : (cartesian_monoidalcat,,
           symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat)
          ⟦ monoidal_cat_tensor_pt z0 x0, y0 ⟧),
    exp_lam_alt (expC x0) f0) x y z f) (identity x)
· (λ x0 : cartesian_monoidalcat,,
          symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat,
   exp_eval_alt (expC x0)) x y = f
 abstract
        (cbn ;
         unfold monoidal_cat_tensor_mor ;
         unfold functoronmorphisms1 ;
         cbn ;
         intros x y z f ;
         refine (_ @ exp_beta_alt (expC _) f) ;
         apply maponpaths_2 ;
         apply prod_lwhisker_rwhisker).
    
C: category
CP: BinProducts C
terminal: Terminal C
expC: Exponentials CP
∏
(x y
 z : cartesian_monoidalcat,,
     symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat)
(g : (cartesian_monoidalcat,,
      symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat) ⟦ z,
     (λ x0 : cartesian_monoidalcat,,
             symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat,
      exp (expC x0)) x y ⟧),
g =
(λ (x0 y0
    z0 : cartesian_monoidalcat,,
         symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat)
 (f : (cartesian_monoidalcat,,
       symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat)
      ⟦ monoidal_cat_tensor_pt z0 x0, y0 ⟧),
 exp_lam_alt (expC x0) f) x y z
  (monoidal_cat_tensor_mor g (identity x)
   · (λ x0 : cartesian_monoidalcat,,
             symmetric_cartesian_monoidalcat,
      exp_eval_alt (expC x0)) x y)
 abstract
        (intros x y z f ; cbn in * ;
         unfold monoidal_cat_tensor_mor ;
         unfold functoronmorphisms1 ;
         cbn ;
         refine (exp_eta_alt (expC _) f @ _) ;
         apply maponpaths ;
         apply maponpaths_2 ;
         refine (!_) ;
         apply prod_lwhisker_rwhisker).
  Defined.
End GeneralConstruction.

  (is_semicartesian_cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV) x
  y =
BinProductPr1 (cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
  (VP x y)

    (VP TV y) (identity TV) 
    (identity y) · BinProductPr2 VC (VP TV y) =
BinProductPr2 VC (VP x y)

     (identity TV) (identity y)
   · BinProductPr2 VC (VP TV y)) =

BinProductArrow VC (VP x (VP y z))
  (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP x y) z)
   · BinProductPr1 VC (VP x y))
  (BinProductArrow VC (VP y z)
     (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP x y) z)
      · BinProductPr2 VC (VP x y))
     (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP x y) z)))

    (make_BinProduct VC (VP y z) x
       (pr11 (VP (VP y z) x)) 
       (pr121 (VP (VP y z) x)) 
       (pr221 (VP (VP y z) x)) 
       (pr2 (VP (VP y z) x)))

          TV) x (VP y z))

    (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP y z) x)
     · BinProductPr1 VC (VP y z))
    (BinProductArrow VC (VP z x)
       (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP y z) x)
        · BinProductPr2 VC (VP y z))
       (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP y z) x)))

    (make_BinProduct VC (VP z x) y

       (pr121 (VP (VP z x) y)) 
       (pr221 (VP (VP z x) y))

expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
x, y, z: V
BinProductArrow VC (VP x (VP y z))
  (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP x y) z)
   · BinProductPr1 VC (VP x y))
  (BinProductArrow VC (VP y z)
     (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP x y) z)
      · BinProductPr2 VC (VP x y))
     (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP x y) z)))
· (BinProductArrow VC
     (make_BinProduct VC 
        (VP y z) x (pr11 (VP (VP y z) x))
        (pr121 (VP (VP y z) x))
        (pr221 (VP (VP y z) x)) 
        (pr2 (VP (VP y z) x)))
     (BinProductPr2 (cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
        (VP x (VP y z)))
     (semi_cart_tensor_pr1
        (is_semicartesian_cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP
           TV) x (VP y z))
   · (BinProductArrow VC 
        (VP y (VP z x))
        (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP y z) x)
         · BinProductPr1 VC (VP y z))
        (BinProductArrow VC 
           (VP z x)
           (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP y z) x)
            · BinProductPr2 VC (VP y z))
           (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP y z) x)))
      · (BinProductPr2
           (cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
           (VP y (VP z x)) · 
         BinProductPr1 VC (VP z x)))) =
BinProductPr2 (cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
  (VP (VP x y) z)

VC: category
TV: Terminal VC
VP: BinProducts VC
expV: Exponentials VP
V:= sym_mon_closed_cartesian_cat VC VP TV expV: sym_mon_closed_cat
x, y, z: V
BinProductArrow VC (VP x (VP y z))
  (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP x y) z)
   · BinProductPr1 VC (VP x y))
  (BinProductArrow VC (VP y z)
     (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP x y) z)
      · BinProductPr2 VC (VP x y))
     (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP x y) z)))
· BinProductArrow VC
    (make_BinProduct VC (VP y z) x
       (pr11 (VP (VP y z) x)) 
       (pr121 (VP (VP y z) x)) 
       (pr221 (VP (VP y z) x)) 
       (pr2 (VP (VP y z) x)))
    (semi_cart_tensor_pr2
       (is_semicartesian_cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP
          TV) x (VP y z))
    (semi_cart_tensor_pr1
       (is_semicartesian_cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP
          TV) x (VP y z))
· BinProductArrow VC (VP y (VP z x))
    (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP y z) x)
     · BinProductPr1 VC (VP y z))
    (BinProductArrow VC (VP z x)
       (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP y z) x)
        · BinProductPr2 VC (VP y z))
       (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP y z) x)))
· BinProductArrow VC
    (make_BinProduct VC (VP z x) y
       (pr11 (VP (VP z x) y)) 
       (pr121 (VP (VP z x) y)) 
       (pr221 (VP (VP z x) y)) 
       (pr2 (VP (VP z x) y)))
    (semi_cart_tensor_pr2
       (is_semicartesian_cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP
          TV) y (VP z x))
    (semi_cart_tensor_pr1
       (is_semicartesian_cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP
          TV) y (VP z x))
· BinProductArrow VC (VP z (VP x y))
    (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP z x) y)
     · BinProductPr1 VC (VP z x))
    (BinProductArrow VC (VP x y)
       (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP z x) y)
        · BinProductPr2 VC (VP z x))
       (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP z x) y)))
· BinProductPr2 VC (VP z (VP x y)) =
BinProductArrow VC
  (make_BinProduct VC z (VP x y)
     (pr11 (VP z (VP x y))) 
     (pr121 (VP z (VP x y))) 
     (pr221 (VP z (VP x y))) 
     (pr2 (VP z (VP x y))))
  (semi_cart_tensor_pr2
     (is_semicartesian_cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
     (VP x y) z)
  (semi_cart_tensor_pr1
     (is_semicartesian_cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
     (VP x y) z) · BinProductPr2 VC (VP z (VP x y))

      · BinProductPr2 VC (VP x y))
     (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP x y) z)))
· (BinProductArrow VC
     (make_BinProduct VC 
        (VP y z) x (pr11 (VP (VP y z) x))
        (pr121 (VP (VP y z) x))
        (pr221 (VP (VP y z) x)) 
        (pr2 (VP (VP y z) x)))
     (BinProductPr2 (cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
        (VP x (VP y z)))
     (BinProductPr1 (cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
        (VP x (VP y z)))
   · (BinProductArrow VC 
        (VP y (VP z x))
        (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP y z) x)
         · BinProductPr1 VC (VP y z))
        (BinProductArrow VC 
           (VP z x)
           (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP y z) x)
            · BinProductPr2 VC (VP y z))
           (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP y z) x)))
      · (BinProductArrow VC
           (make_BinProduct VC 
              (VP z x) y 
              (pr11 (VP (VP z x) y))
              (pr121 (VP (VP z x) y))
              (pr221 (VP (VP z x) y))
              (pr2 (VP (VP z x) y)))
           (BinProductPr2
              (cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
              (VP y (VP z x)))
           (BinProductPr1
              (cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
              (VP y (VP z x)))
         · BinProductArrow VC 
             (VP x y)
             (BinProductPr1 VC (VP (VP z x) y)
              · BinProductPr2 VC (VP z x))
             (BinProductPr2 VC (VP (VP z x) y))))) =
BinProductPr1 (cartesian_monoidalcat VC VP TV)
  (VP (VP x y) z)
